### [210] [Disentangling Continuous-Time Latent Dynamics: Identifiability of Latent SDEs via Diffusion Shifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28228)
*Yuanyuan Wang,Wenjie Wang,Haoxuan Li,Mingming Gong,Kun Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了连续时间潜在随机微分方程（SDE）模型的可识别性问题，利用环境引起的扩散协方差偏移，证明了在无需漂移稀疏性假设的情况下，潜在坐标可在置换和缩放意义下被识别，并提出了两阶段估计方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离散时间潜在因果模型已建立较强的可识别性结果，但连续时间潜在SDE模型的可识别性仍 largely open，本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 研究加性噪声潜在SDE模型，假设共享漂移但环境特异性扩散协方差。首先证明线性Ornstein-Uhlenbeck系统的可识别性，再推广至一般加性噪声SDE。提出基于环境诱导扩散协方差偏移的两阶段估计器，用于潜在解缠和可选的因果图恢复。

Result: 两个具有成对坐标方差比不同的对角扩散机制足以在置换和缩放意义下识别潜在坐标；在温和光滑性下，瞬时漂移-雅可比因果图可识别至相同置换。合成系统实验验证了理论识别边界，Hardanger Bridge监测数据展示了实际应用效果。

Conclusion: 本文建立了连续时间潜在SDE模型的可识别性理论，无需漂移稀疏性假设，并通过实验验证了方法的有效性。

Abstract: Causal representation learning for time series has developed strong identifiability results in discrete-time latent causal models, but identifiability in continuous-time latent stochastic differential equation (SDE) models remains largely open. We address this gap using environment-induced shifts in diffusion covariance. We study additive-noise latent SDEs observed through an unknown nonlinear diffeomorphism, with shared drift but environment-specific diffusion covariance. We show that two diagonal diffusion regimes with pairwise distinct coordinate-wise variance ratios identify the latent coordinates up to permutation and scaling, without any sparsity assumption on the drift. We first prove this result for linear Ornstein--Uhlenbeck systems and then extend it to general additive-noise latent SDEs. Under mild smoothness, the instantaneous drift-Jacobian causal graph is identifiable up to the same permutation. We propose a two-stage estimator for latent disentanglement and optional graph recovery; experiments on synthetic systems confirm the predicted identifiability boundary, and an application to Hardanger Bridge monitoring data illustrates the approach on real sensor trajectories.

</details>


### [211] [Parameter Efficient Hybrid Transformer (PEHT) for Network Traffic Prediction via Dynamic Urban Congestion Integration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28274)
*Abdolazim Rezaei,Mehdi Sookhak,Mahboobeh Haghparast*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出PEHT框架，通过LoRA高效微调和多模态融合策略，将城市移动性与拥塞信息融入Transformer架构，显著提升蜂窝网络流量预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 网络流量预测对动态城市蜂窝网络的资源分配至关重要，但由于复杂移动模式、拥塞动态和异构用户行为的影响，预测仍面临挑战。

Method: 提出参数高效混合Transformer（PEHT），分离主要网络通信特征与次要城市移动性特征；在Transformer编码器中引入LoRA减少可训练参数；采用多模态融合策略将外部移动性和拥塞特征注入解码器以改进预测。

Result: 在Telecom Italia Milan数据集和多个合成拥塞场景上，PEHT在RMSE、MAE和R²指标上均优于现有最先进基线。

Conclusion: PEHT通过参数高效设计和多模态信息融合，有效提升了城市蜂窝网络流量预测的准确性和效率。

Abstract: Accurate network traffic prediction is a critical element for efficient resource allocation in dynamic urban cellular networks. However, prediction remains challenging because network demand is influenced by complex mobility patterns, congestion dynamics, and heterogeneous user behavior. This paper introduces the Parameter-Efficient Hybrid Transformer (PEHT), a network traffic prediction framework that integrates urban mobility and congestion information into a Transformer-based architecture. PEHT separates primary network communication features from secondary urban mobility features and incorporates Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) into the Transformer encoder to reduce the number of trainable parameters while maintaining high predictive accuracy. A multimodal fusion strategy then injects external mobility and congestion features into the decoder to improve traffic forecasting. Experiments on the Telecom Italia Milan dataset and multiple synthetic congestion scenarios show that PEHT outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in terms of RMSE, MAE, and $R^2$. The implementation is available in the GitHub repository.

</details>


### [212] [Towards Automating Scientific Review with Google's Paper Assistant Tool](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28277)
*Rajesh Jayaram,Drew Tyler,David Woodruff,Corinna Cortes,Yossi Matias,Vahab Mirrokni,Vincent Cohen-Addad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为PAT（论文辅助工具）的AI代理框架，用于深度科学评审与验证，能够将数学错误检测的召回率提升34%，并已在STOC和ICML会议上作为预提交工具部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI加速科学发现导致传统同行评审无法规模化，亟需AI来加速验证和评审过程以缓解这一矛盾。

Method: 提出四级AI-人类协作分类法；开发PAT代理框架，利用推理缩放技术对完整科学稿件进行全面评估，包括理论验证、实验检查、改进建议和缺陷识别。

Result: 在SPOT基准测试中，PAT对数学错误的零样本召回率提升了34%；在STOC和ICML会议上部署后，能够识别关键错误并提出实质性改进建议。

Conclusion: PAT能早期捕获错误，减轻评审员认知负担，同时保留评审员对评审结果的控制权，是迈向AI辅助科学评审体系的重要一步。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence is driving a revolution in scientific discovery, accelerating everything from hypothesis generation to mathematical theorem proving. However, this rapid acceleration is creating a systemic challenge: traditional human peer review cannot scale to match the influx of AI-assisted science. Ultimately, to resolve this tension, we must also deploy AI to accelerate the verification and review process itself. To frame the discussion around this transition, we propose a taxonomy consisting of four progressive levels of AI-human collaboration in scientific evaluation, and discuss various trade-offs involved with each.
  As a step toward this future, we introduce the Paper Assistant Tool (PAT), an agentic AI framework built for deep scientific review and verification. PAT ingests full scientific manuscripts and produces a comprehensive evaluation, checking theoretical results, validating experiments, suggesting improvements, and identifying potential flaws. By utilizing inference scaling techniques, PAT is able to identify deeper issues than a single model call alone, achieving a 34% improvement over zero-shot recall on mathematical errors in the SPOT benchmark. Pilot deployments of PAT as a pre-submission tool for authors at two major Computer Science conferences -- STOC and ICML -- demonstrate its ability to identify critical errors and suggest substantive improvements to research papers. By catching errors early, PAT eases the cognitive burden placed on referees, while preserving their control over the outcomes of the review process.

### [213] [Democratic ICAI: Debating Our Way to Steering Principles from Preferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28294)
*Kevin Kingslin,Anish Natekar,Ashutosh Ranjan,Vivek Srivastava,Savita Bhat,Shirish Karande*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 民主逆宪法AI（Democratic ICAI）通过结构化角色辩论生成多竞争性理由，从偏好中提取更全面的指导原则，提升了偏好预测的准确性和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的基于偏好的对齐方法难以捕捉人类判断背后的推理过程，成对标签只揭示最终选择而非形成偏好的考量因素。现有方法如逆宪法AI（ICAI）虽然通过自然语言原则提升可解释性，但单次解释遗漏了复杂决策中的细微差别。

Method: 提出Democratic ICAI方法，通过结构化角色辩论收集多个竞争性理由，从而更广泛地表达影响每个比较的因素。从这些更丰富的信号中推导出更清晰、更全面的指导原则，并用于指导基于LLM和决策树的判断模型。

Result: 在创意偏好基准MuCE-Pref和LiTBench上的多个创意任务类别中，Democratic ICAI产生了更忠实的偏好结构，相比深思提示和基于原则的基线方法，提高了跨任务的平均偏好预测准确率，且生成的宪法被LLM标注者更偏好。

Conclusion: Democratic ICAI通过多角色辩论机制有效增强了偏好对齐的可解释性和预测能力，为复杂决策场景中的偏好建模提供了更细致和忠实的方法。

Abstract: Preference-based alignment often struggles to capture the reasoning that underlies human judgments. Many evaluations rely on multiple interacting criteria, yet pairwise labels reveal only the final choice rather than the considerations that shape preferences. Inverse Constitutional AI (ICAI) improves interpretability in decision making by summarizing preferences into natural-language principles, but its single-pass explanations miss much of the nuance involved in complex decisions. We introduce Democratic ICAI, a novel approach that gathers multiple competing rationales through structured persona debate, offering a broader and more expressive account of the factors influencing each comparison. From these richer signals, we derive clearer and more comprehensive steering principles and use them to guide decision modeling through both LLM-based and decision-tree judges. Experiments on creative preference benchmarks, MuCE-Pref and LiTBench, across multiple creative task categories show that Democratic ICAI yields a more faithful preference structure. It improves average preference prediction across tasks relative to deliberative prompting and principle-based baselines, while producing constitutions that LLM annotators prefer.

### [214] [VGB for Masked Diffusion Model: Efficient Test-time Scaling for Reward Satisfaction and Sample Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28301)
*Kijung Jeon,Thuy-Duong Vuong,Molei Tao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出MDM-VGB，一种将掩码扩散模型与基于奖励的重新掩码相结合的离散扩散采样器，在满足约束条件和优化下游奖励方面表现优异，理论上具有对噪声的鲁棒性和二次复杂度，实验证明在数独和QM9等任务上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理时扩展（inference-time scaling）是提升生成模型性能的有效范式，尤其在输出需要满足结构约束或优化下游奖励的场景中。现有方法如best-of-N采样因错误累积导致指数级复杂度，缺乏理论保障，因此亟需一种既有效又具有理论保证的奖励引导生成方法。

Method: 基于掩码扩散模型（MDM），借鉴Jerrum-Sinclair回溯马尔可夫链的成功，将回溯随机游走从固定前缀树扩展到掩码状态图，允许任意位置上的掩码与重新掩码操作。算法偏好那些能导向更高价值部分配置的移动，从而实现高奖励生成和低奖励样本的高效修复。

Result: 理论证明MDM-VGB对过程验证器噪声具有鲁棒性，且计算复杂度为二次（O(N²)），而best-of-N等启发式方法因错误累积呈指数复杂度。实验上，在数独和QM9等约束满足与科学基准任务中展示了优异的实证性能。

Conclusion: MDM-VGB通过结合理论严谨的回溯机制与掩码扩散模型，为奖励引导的离散生成提供了一种高效且鲁棒的解决方案，在复杂约束任务中显著优于传统测试时启发式方法。

Abstract: Inference-time scaling is a promising paradigm to improve generative models, especially when outputs must satisfy structural constraints or optimize downstream rewards. We consider Masked Diffusion Model (MDM) and introduce MDM-VGB, a discrete diffusion sampler that augments unmasking generation with theoretically principled reward-guided remasking. Inspired by the recent success of the classical Jerrum-Sinclair backtracking Markov chain in reward-tilted generation, MDM-VGB extends the backtracking random walk from a fixed prefix tree to a masked-state graph, allowing tokens to be unmasked and remasked at arbitrary positions. The resulting sampler favors unmasking and remasking moves that lead to higher-value partial configurations, enabling both effective high-reward generation and efficient repair of low-reward samples. We prove that MDM-VGB is robust to process-verifier noise and achieves quadratic complexity, while popular test-time heuristics such as best-of-$N$ can incur exponential complexity due to error accumulation. Our theoretical findings are corroborated by strong empirical performance, particularly on popular constraint-satisfaction and scientific benchmarks such as Sudoku and QM9.

</details>
